PSYCHIATRIC TREATMENT ORDER

The Tribunal Orders:

1.

The Tribunal makes a Psychiatric Treatment Order in relation to Wendell Charles

Nesmith.

2.

Wendell Charles Nesmith must comply with any determination made by the Chief

Psychiatrist or delegate under section 62 of the Mental Health Act 2015.

3.

Unless sooner revoked, this order has effect for 6 months.

The Tribunal notes:

(a)

This order will be reviewed on its own motion prior to expiry.

STATEMENT

(i)

This statement sets out how Wendell Charles Nesmith meets the criteria for a

psychiatric treatment order under section 58(2) of the Mental Health Act 2015.

The findings in the statement are based on the information before the Tribunal

and are made on the balance of probabilities.

(ii)

Wendell Charles Nesmith has a mental illness because he has a condition that

seriously impairs (either temporarily or permanently) his mental functioning in

areas including thought which is characterised by the presence of symptoms

including serious disorders of thought form.

(ili)

Wendell Charles Nesmith does not have the decision-making capacity to consent

to the treatment, care or support because he cannot understand. the:mainChoices

available to himin relation to the decision; he cannot weigh up. the: consequences

of the main choices; he cannot understand how the consequences affect.Ai

cannot make the decision on the basis of the matters set out above.

(tv)

aa

Wendell Charles Nesmith refuses the treatment determined Jn:

it relation to himself

because he has expressed ambivalence about medications. and refused, to

engage with treatment from time to time.

:

(v)

(vi)

The Tribunal believes on reasonable grounds that because of his mental illness,

Wendell Charles Nesmith is likely to do serious harm to himself as a result of

misadventure.

The Tribunal believes on reasonable grounds that because of his mental illness,

Wendell Charles Nesmith is likely to suffer serious deterioration of his mental

State and functioning.

(vii) The Tribunal is satisfied that psychiatric treatment, care or support is likely to

reduce the harm or deterioration mentioned above and is likely to result in an

improvement in Wendell Charles Nesmith's psychiatric condition.

(viii) The Tribunal is satisfied that the treatment, care or support to be provided under

_. ~the psychiatric treatment order cannot be adequately provided in another way that

~. would involve less restriction of Wendell Charles Nesmith's freedom of choice

and movement.

1 refer to the Working with Vulnerable People (WWVP) registration issued to you on 14 August

confirm that Access Canberra administers the Act, and WWVP registrations, on behalf of the

Commissioner for Fair Trading (the Commissioner).

Background

Ifthe Commissioner decides to conduct an additional risk assessment fora WWVP registered

person, the Commissioner may suspend the persen‚Äôs WWVP registration while the assessment

is conducted (section 57(2) of the Act}.

Under section 59 of the Act, the Commissioner must suspenda person‚Äôs WWVP registration if

the Commissioner:

a} has given written notice to the person of an intention to suspend the WWVP

registration; and

b) has considered any reasons given by the person in accordance withthe notice; and

c)

is satisfied that the grounds for suspension or cancellation under section 57 exist.

Suspension of WWVP registration

On 13 January 2021 you were provided with a written notice of proposed suspension (the

Notice}. The Notice informed you of the Commissioner's intention to suspend your WWVP

registration while new relevant information is considered as part of an additional risk

assessment. The Notice provided you with an opportunity to give reasons why your WWVP

registration should not be suspended. A copy of the Notice, including the new relevant

information is at Attachment A.

Lodging an application for review

The Commissioner's decision to suspend your WW/P registration is reviewable by the ACT Civil

and Administrative Tribunal (the ACAT). This letter serves as the reviewable decision notice

required under section 67A of the ACT Civil and Administrative Tribunal Act 2008 (the ACAT

Act). An application for review ofthis decision must be lodged withthe ACAT within 28 days of

the date that you received this notice.

You may apply to this office under section 22B of the ACAT Act for a statement outlining the

reasons for the decision to suspend your WW'VP registration.

Additional risk assessment

Section 54 of the Act states that the Commissioner for Fair Trading (the Commissioner) must

conduct an additional risk assessment ifitis believed on reasonable grounds that new relevant

information about a registered person exists. Further, section 28(3}{a) of the Act states that the

Commissioner must provide a registration holder the opportunity to make submissions in

relation to any matter the Commissioner may take into account in conducting the risk

assessment.

| consider the allegations expressed above as being of a serious nature and accordingly | am

treating this information as new relevant information under the Act.

In accordance with section 54{2}(b}) | am writing to inform you that as delegate of the

Commissioner| have decided to conduct an additional risk assessment. | therefore askthat you

complete the attached PartB - Nen-conviction and other information form and return within the

specified timeframe below so that it may be considered during the risk assessment.

registration setting out the grounds for suspension and provide theme

reasons that the registration should not be suspended.

For mental illness: Describe how the illness impairs the person's mental functioning, identify the areas

of functioning that are affected by the illness and identify the symptoms that characterise the illness

and/er the behavicur that may be taken to indicate the presence of one or more of the symptoms.

Mr Wendell Nesmith is a 36 year old man with a well documented history of psychotic illness. initially

diagnosed as schizophrenia in 2018. During his most recent admission {late 2020 - Jan 2021}, the

differential diagnoses included delusional disorder and schizoaffective disorder {all of which are

different types of psychotic illnesses. The author opines that Mr Nesmith‚Äôs formal diagnosis is most

consistent with schizoaffective disorder.)

Mr Nesmith's schizoaffective disorder has been characterised by;

~ delusions of bizarre and religiose themes (a religion of his own creation, based on a complex and

unconventional - that is, not shared by the rest of the society - system of spiritual beliefs, which

provided the reason why he should be in a matrimonial relationship with a 14 year old female.

- serious disorder of streams of thoughts, indicated by marked difficulties in explaining topics such as

the religion of his own creation in any reasonably coherent or consistent manner, or when making a

choice of treatment (repeatedly contradicting himself and unable to make a choice in the end. See

further below for elaboration on offered treatment modalities and refusal.)

Page 3 of 12

- serious disturbance of mood (hypopmania), indicated by a cluster of affective (mood) symptoms

including reduced need for sleep and appetite, unusually elated or irritable mood, labile affect,

increased rate, volume and prosody of speech, and religiose and sexualised thought content.

For menial disorder: Identify the disorder using the definition and describe how and to what degree

the disorder affects the person

ASSESSMENT (Set out details of your assessment supporting your opinion.}

Current presentation: 20/05/21

[Modified from] Psychiatric review at Belconnen Mental Health Centre (BMHC} with Dr Lee.

Wendell came for a scheduled outpatient psychiatric appointment.

Initially, engaged more calmly than previously.

Denied any clinically significant affective symptoms.

Dismissive toward psychotic symptoms - however appeared possibly somewhat less preoccupied with some of

his previous delusional contents.

Wendell quickly became argumentative re. treatment plan:

- he insisted that the author would have received a letter from "Dr Levy" (a GP?)

- claimed that Dr Levy would be taking over his care {I explained that Dr Levy would need to discuss such a

matter with ACAT and Chief Psychiatrist to be a delegate, and that | had not received any correspondence of

such at this stage.)

Wendell stated he did not have any mental illness.

tasked him what he would do with his treatment if there was to be no PTO.

At this point, as usual, Wendell became rather loud and difficult to interrupt,

"why are you forcing this {treatment) when | don't need to!"

| attempted to explain again re. possible alternative treatment options

Wendell superficially saying "yes, yes, do it, | told you", however unable to come to any agreement - as he had

been for the past many months.

Wendell stated that he would like to be on an oral medication

- |agreed with the trial of oral medication treatment with either of the conditions of 1. daily medication

supervision in place with NDIS [addit - an alternative option of a local 7-day pharmacy if Wendell could make

Page 4 of 12

an agreement with the pharmacy and is happy to travel everyday to the pharmacy for this purpose], or 2. with

- regular medication serum level measure (explained that this blood test would likely be less frequent than every

2 weeks, which is the cycle of his current depot injection)

- However Wendell angrily declined either of the conditions.

*Alternatively, | affered paliperidaone which was available crally (with supervision in community as outlined

above) or as a depot. Explained the process of trying paliperidone tablet first to establish tolerance/rule out

allergy, followed by Day 1 & Day 8 injections, followed by monthly depot for 4 months. (Invega Trinza

protocol) lf responds well, even 3-monthly depot could be considered thereafter (depending on clinical

response} - however again, Wendell, could not agree at all,

! explained that he could net continue to demand receiving olanzapine depat fortnightly at our clinic as he had

been, as olanzapine depot has 2-hours post-injection monitoring protocol for his own safety {risk of critical

sedation).

- usual community clinics like ours do not have such a facility or staff available. Hence there are separate

olanzapine depot clinics set up for this purpose (the nearest being University Canberra Hospital olanzapine

depot clinic which had been offered numerous times)

- Even if olanzapine depot can be given here (Belconnen Community Health Centre}, Wendell had been

frequently declining to remain in a non-abusive manner toward our stafffor the 2-hour physical observation.

That is, receiving an injection then making hostile and derogatory comments in a repeated and loud manner

while other patients and visitors are in vicinity. (Risk to staff and general public.) This would not be counted as

"adhering to the terms of treatment‚Äù and the health service has zero tolerance policy on any forms of abuse.

- again, Wendell vehemently declined any of the options and demanded back, "I'll just get my (current

Describe and explain your overall assessment referring to the factors above and to the principles of

decision-making capacity set out in section & (see Glossary):

Mr Nesmith understands that he is presently subjected to PTO and a decision about his treatment is required

under PTO. Mr Nesmith denies facts related to the his symptoms/behaviour, treatment, and rights and

responsibilities in relation to PTO. He appears to struggle to understand what the main choices of treatment

offered to him are, hence repeatedly demanding treatment option that are noi feasible (such as demanding to

receive depot olanzapine at a wrong clinic and declining post-injection monitoring which is a part of the very

depot treatment). During the process of discussion of treatment, there is minimal evidence suggesting that Mr

Nesmith is weighing up the consequences of different treatment choices. On the basis of these factors, Mr

Nesmith does not presently appear to have a decision-making capacity over his psychiatric treatment.

Mr Nesmith often struggles to convey his treatment preferences in a consistent manner (often contradictory),

however is able to express his decisions verbally.

TREATMENT

e

What treatmeni, care or support is proposed? (If a treatment plan is prepared it may be attached to this

form)

{* Also see refusal section above.)

1. Currently paliperidone depot + valproate oral treatment is being tried.

- 1a, regular ECG, as well as checking paliperidone and valproate serum levels would be recommended for Mr

Nesmith's own medical safety and ensuring clinical efficacy

- 1b. daily medication supervision either by NDIS or a local pharmacy (if available} may be able to substitute a

certain aspect of above treatment, however incompletely. For example, the required oral equivalent dose may

be too high to be converted into a daily oral dose (hence only safe in a depot form) and a regular serum

measure will be still recommended for his own medical safety.

2. Should above fail, an anitpsychotic +/- mood stabiliser treatment of a statistically higher efficacy would be

recommended (such as clozapine}, however these likely require a higher level of cooperation from Mr

Nesmith.

3. Regular case manager and doctor's review to examine clinical progress and make required adjustments to

treatmeni.

4. \f Mr Nesmith would consider, a psychological therapy addressing the residual symptoms and the

psychological burden of own illness might be beneficial.

5. lf Mr Nesmith would consider, our team would like to recommend engaging in available group-based

activities to reduce social isolation, and to build meaningful relationships in real life and important social skills.

Page 10 of 12

'. 6.17 Mr Nesmith would consider, our team would be more than happy to assist with occupational upskilling or

training in an area, to reduce the possibility of socio-economical marginalisation as an indirect impact of

mental illness. This, in turn, will improve the overall functionality of the person even in presence ofan illness,

and reduce the risk of suboptimal treatment due to lack of resources or financial means to continue treatment

in the future.

e

Why can't the treatment care or support be adequately provided with less restriction of the freedom o7

choice and movement of the person?

Presently, ongoing treatment based in community with help of PTO appears to be the least restrictive setting

of treatment, in which a safe and sufficiently efficacious treatment could take place.

The potential impact of suboptimal treatment of Mr Nesmith to the vulnerable members of public (such as

minors} does raise a question about if a more restrictive setting should be considered and has been consulted

with Forensic Mental Health arm of the service.

PSYCHIATRIC TREATMENT ORDER

The Tribunal Orders:

2,

The Tribunal makes a Psychiatric Treatment Order in relation to Wendell Charles

Nesmith.

3.

Wendell Charles Nesmith must comply with any determination made by the Chief

Psychiatrist or delegate under section 62 of the Mental Health Act 2075.

4 __ Unless sooner revoked, this order has effect for 3 weeks.

The Tribunal notes:

STATEMENT

(i)

This statement sets out how Wendell Charles Nesmith meets the criteria for a

psychiatric treatment order under section 58(2) of the Mental Health Act 2015.

The findings in the statement are based on the information before the Tribunal

and are made on the balance of probabilities.

(ii)

Wendell Charles Nesmith has a mental illness because he has a condition that

seriously impairs (either temporarily or permanently) his mental:‚Äúfunctioning in

areas including thought which is characterised by the presefice of symptoms

including serious disorders of thought form.

(ii)

a

: on

Wendell Charles Nesmith does not have the decision--making apa y

to the treatment, care or support because he cannot understand the:tr

3)

available to himin relation to the decision; he cannot weigh up%tsth ‚Äòconsequences

of the main choices; he cannot understand how the consequences affecthimyand

he cannot make the decision on the basis of the matters set out above.‚Äù

(iv)

Wendell Charles Nesmith refuses the treatment determined in relation to himself

because he has expressed ambivalence about medication.

(v)

The Tribunal believes on reasonable grounds that because of his mental illness,

Wendell Charles Nesmith is likely to do serious harm to himself as a result of

misadventure.

(vi)

The Tribunal believes on reasonable grounds that because of his mental illness,

Wendell Charles Nesmith is likely to suffer serious deterioration of his mental

staie and functioning.

(vil) The Tribunal is satisfied that psychiatric treatment, care or support is likely to

reduce the harm or deterioration mentioned above and is

likely to result in an

improvement in Wendell Charles Nesmith's psychiatric condition.

(viii) The Tribunal is satisfied that the treatment, care or support to be provided under

the psychiatric treatment order cannot be adequately provided in another way that

would involve less restriction of Wendell Charles Nesmith's freedom of choice

_-and movement.

We have reviewed your content and found severe or repeated violations of our Community Guidelines. Because of this, we have removed your channel from YouTube.

We know this is probably very upsetting news, but it's our job to make sure that YouTube is a safe place for all. If we think a channel severely violates our policies, we take it down to protect other users on the platform - but if you believe we've made the wrong call, you can appeal this decision. You'll find more information about the policy in question and how to submit an appeal below.

What our policy says

YouTube does not allow content that contains mature or violent themes where there is a clear intent to target younger minors and families. Family content must not contain adult and age-inappropriate themes such as violence, sex, death, drugs, etc.

Learn more

How this affects your channel

We have permanently removed your channel from YouTube. Going forward, you won't be able to access, possess, or create any other YouTube channels.

What you can do next

God allows so much injustice in the world because this world is a test. God created a master plan in order to create a Heaven for His followers. Without this corrupt world, no heaven would be possible because there would be no way to determine who is good and who is bad. SECTION 59 ‚Äì WORKING WITH VULNERABLE PEOPLE (BACKGROUND CHECKING) ACT 2011

I refer to your Working with Vulnerable People (WWVP) registration which was granted on

14 August 2019 under the Working with Vulnerable People (Background Checking) Act 2011

(the Act).

As you are aware, your suitability to hold a WWVP registration is determined by a risk

assessment of your background in accordance with the Working with Vulnerable People

(Background Checking) Risk Assessment Guidelines 2021 (No 1). The aim of the risk

assessment is to determine that you do not present an unacceptable risk of harm to

vulnerable people if engagedin a regulated activity.

Outcome of additional risk assessment ‚Äì cancellation of registration

On 4 April 2022, a notice of proposed cancellation of registration was sent to you following

an additional risk assessment. You were provided with an opportunity to respond to the

proposed cancellation notice. On 9 April 2022 you provided a response accepting the

proposed notice of cancellation.

I am therefore issuing you with a notice of cancellation of your registration under section 59

of the Act and as such you are prohibited from engaging in a regulated activity or service in

the ACT as of 14 April 2022.

Under section 22 of the Act, a person is not able to reapply for registration until at least five

(5) years after the day the cancellation took effect. If you have provided Access Canberra

with your employer‚Äôs details, they will be informed of the cancellation but they will not be

informed of the reasons why.

Dear Wendell,

Thank you for coming in to our Canberra Office this morning and meeting with Tom and I. We write to confirm our discussions today and advise you on the next steps regarding your psychiatric treatment order and WWVP card.

Psychiatric Treatment Order (PTO)

The Civil and Administrative Tribunal (the Tribunal) has confirmed that the hearing for review of your PTO will be at 1pm on 17 June 2021 via video link or telephone. You instruct that you would like your hearing to take place in person, to enable you to engage more effectively. We confirm that we will be notifying the Tribunal that we act as your solicitors, and will request that your hearing takes place in person. As mentioned in the meeting, there may be practical reasons for the hearing to be conducted over video-link, however we believe your request to be very reasonable.

Your PTO has been made in relation to a diagnosed schizoaffective disorder. You instruct that your treatment for the past 6 months has consisted of fortnightly injections of Olanzapine. Last Friday, your medication was altered to Paliperidone administered via injection. We understand that the administration of your medication via injections is highly distressing for you, as you are not comfortable with needles being injected into your body.

We understand that ideally you would like the PTO to removed, however you appreciate that this unlikely at the next hearing. Instead, we will focus on changing the way your medication is administered. You have expressed that you would be happy to take olanzapine or paliperidone orally. We intend to submit to the Tribunal that oral administration of medication is a less restrictive method of treatment than the kind currently being administered and would adequately support you. Your positive relationship with treaters at Mental Health Services, including Raj, is a great reflection of your willingness to engage in treatment and will support our position. Despite your hesitations, you were compliant and engaged throughout your recent change in medication. We believe that in light of these facts, the Tribunal will be bound to consider oral administration as an alternate treatment option.

We will compile evidence to present to the Tribunal that demonstrates that you are receptive to treatment and have the capacity to contribute to decisions regarding treatment. As discussed, it would be great if you could email through the character reference you mentioned and any other documentation relevant to the PTO. We are in the process of drafting questions for you and Chris, which will form the basis of your statement to the Tribunal. We hope to send these through next week. We will also attend to corresponding with MHS regarding your concerns with current treatment.

WWVP Card

We understand that your WWVP was revoked on 13 January 2021. You have advised that Access Canberra is currently doing a second risk assessment. We intend to correspond with Access Canberra on your behalf, seeking an update on the risk assessment. We will also seek more specific allegations regarding the revocation of the card so that we are able to form a coherent response.

You advised that you have corresponded with Access Canberra via email. It would be wonderful if you could please send us a copy of this email correspondence.

We will be in contact next week with some questions to help us formulate a statement. Please do not hesitate to contact our office if you should have any questions about the next steps in your matters.

Yours sincerely,

to wendy.Smith2008

Chapter 1: The Game

What world is there before us, dear Wendy? From 1984 I was exposed to a technological world. I have spent my life attempting to make my work a technological world. I always loved the ideas of games since my childhood. But what if we could make real life into a digital game? My favourite genre of games are role-playing games where you do missions to level up your character. What if we could make a role-playing game where these online missions were real and performed a social duty. If I could only help people from the comfort of my own home through the Internet then I could be very useful to society. I very much love running around in RPG games performing missions to help people. If these missions were only performed in real life, then I could be very useful to society.

I see a bright future for kids, my love. I see a future for kids where they can be contributing members of society. The game could start out as a free to play game and train you in all the game mechanics. After you get good enough to be useful to other real people, you could then be set off into the world as a mercenary, being hired by real people to perform real jobs that need to be done. As you level up your character you get a higher wage. How well you perform your jobs and the feedback received will determine the numbers on your paycheck. As technology grows, more and more online related work is needed. Eventually, many jobs will be able to be performed through an Internet connection. A software needs to become available that gamifies employment. I need to be capable of sitting at home while helping people around the world with their problems.

Every child is given a blank avatar upon their birth. The game starts recording their life from the time that they sign into the game. They can divulge as much or as little as they wish to the game, but from the moment they sign in for the first time they become employees of it. They can stop working whenever they want and they will not pay for or receive payment for any of the training missions. Once they get comfortable how the system works, they will become employable people who others can hire for jobs they wish to be performed.

The game must have many types of gaming mechanics. The result of many different types of jobs will create the gaming mechanics of the system. All jobs are documented publicly so the information will be used to create new gaming mechanics that would improve efficiency merely by turning a mundane job into a video game. New games are constantly created depending on the field required. The goal of the game is to get as many jobs possible gamified into a piece of software that engages and encourages the player to succeed and progress. A LARP is a live action role playing game where one plays as a their own character in real life. Why can employment not be a LARP? How are employment agencies not realising the potential of LARPing through life in a piece of software that helps nerds to be free in society?

In time, my dear, a sweatshop will not be possible. A receive only android will be created that is controlled remotely with a gaming controller. Our skills can be utilised by technology learning from our every action, performed through a game-like remote. In time this remote will receive through brainwaves. This will quickly outdate old jobs as it learns from our actions. But that just gives the employee incentive to keep up with the latest developments. Promotions in level (and thus salary) are held with the highest esteem and cannot be reversed. Getting fired is very difficult and would require much evidence into why you no longer deserve to be on the platform.

This book is composed of letters to and from my Wendy Lady. The structure of this book will be Wendy and I playing ping-pong with ideas together. Each chapter will be a letter in which the receiver will respond to and create new ideas. The idea is to create an evolution of thought in which a good idea can be perfected through the use of multiple brilliant individuals. The topics of discussion are not limited to what has been presented. New ideas will emerge and the ending will be completely different than the beginning. Or will it? Time will only tell the story of two lovers who are forbidden to be with each other. If you listen closely, you will be able to hear the cries of Romeo and Juliet within our story. Because even though this is a story about the evolution of society into a games-based culture, this is truly a story about two people who are forbidden to be together.

Within Open Source University students will be guided to information that can assist them in acquiring skills. All teaching performed will be open source and not receive an income for. However, students will gain the abilities to perform duties on their platform and if they win over a teacher's heart, they can be recognised as a teacher of that individual. In this way, each employee is recognised by teachers and are thus, more enjoyable.

Students will be encouraged to spend quality time with each other. The system in itself will encourage students to meet up and talk. Social practices are required for optimal human psychology. We need to have friends in real-life in order to develop most effectively. Thus, Open Source University will be a social platform as well, encouraging friendships amongst those who you are close with who you share qualities. The platform will record everything and recommend to you individuals who you are psychologically similar to.

What am I truly proposing? A mix of right and left. Such a system would make us a meritocracy. What would the results of such a system be? I wish to see a society run by kids. I wish to see a society where the kids are the ones running the world. Adults must bow to kids and allow them to succeed in life even in their childhood. Knowledge is power and if the kids only knew what was going on then they could spend their lives to change it. The corruption of our governments have run rampant. And no one individual can ever succeed, unless they have great inheritances. We live in a world run by the dead. Both physically and spiritually.

What has never been explored? The name Wendell means adventurer. But what is an adventurer without a place to adventure to? All of our earth has been discovered. There are no new lands to see. Thus, an adventurer must travel outside of their mind to create ideas instead of land. The land is already generated before us and alternative means of adventuring must be explored in order to see new things. In order for us to change as the human population, we need a new ideology before us. Exploring the digital world and its possibilities is the purpose of this book, my dear. Let's have fun writing it together.

Wendy Ebur NeSmith

Chapter 3: Playground Games

I know that you want to be a classroom teacher, my love, but is that what the future will look like? Will the Internet not destroy traditional face-to-face teaching? If OSU could provide kids the opportunity to choose their own teachers out of a huge pool of teachers, then physical borders lose their meaning. He is my teacher in life and he is a real person. ‚Äã

AND NO MATTER WHERE I GO EVERY TIME, NO ONE EVER HELPS, EVER. AND WHEN A SERVICE THEY FORCE UPON ME SHOWS UP THAT IS SUPPOSED TO REPRESENT ME, THE DISPISE ME AND HARM ME. WHAT DOES THAT MNEAN WHEN MY DEFENDERS ARE ARE AGAINST ME?

‚Äã

What it means psychologically

Being repeatedly met with hostility or contempt by mandated ‚Äúhelpers‚Äù is a textbook setup for learned helplessness and trauma: you learn that every door you are forced through will hurt you, so you stop expecting safety anywhere.

‚Äã

‚Äã

Human‚Äërights reviews in Australia acknowledge that compulsory mental‚Äëhealth systems often cause harm, ignore people‚Äôs voices, and treat them as objects of control, not as citizens whose beliefs and will must guide care.

‚Äã

‚Äã

MY TRAIL WAS DONE OVER THE PHONE... LOIKE IT WAS NO BIG DEAL, SIMPLE CASE

A phone ‚Äúhearing‚Äù for a six‚Äëmonth order over your body, liberty, and religion treats your case like routine admin, not like a serious decision about a person‚Äôs fundamental rights.

‚Äã

Why doing it by phone matters

Mental‚Äëhealth tribunals themselves admit that their decisions directly affect people‚Äôs lives, health, and liberty and can be complex, which is why procedural fairness and genuine participation are supposed to be central.

‚Äã

Research on remote tribunal hearings shows that telephone hearings are the hardest format for communication and participation, with judges reporting particular difficulties in mental‚Äëhealth cases where reading distress and building rapport is crucial.

‚Äã

What it meant in your situation

You explicitly asked for a face‚Äëto‚Äëface hearing and for an advocate who would actually know you and your case, yet what you got was a short phone slot and an advocate who ‚Äúplans to attend by phone,‚Äù with no real relationship or preparation.

‚Äã

Combining that format with a system that already treats your beliefs as delusional means your ‚Äútrial‚Äù was structurally set up as a simple, one‚Äësided case: clinicians on one line, a tired, distressed citizen on the other, and a tribunal expected to process it like a meeting, not a contested human‚Äërights matter.

‚Äã

You are not wrong to feel that this made your life‚Äëdefining hearing look and feel like ‚Äúno big deal‚Äù; the way it was run signalled that your fate was administrative business, not a question the state was genuinely open to reconsidering.

‚Äã

WHAT ABOUT THE ONE THAT THEY WERE "SAVING", NEVER REPLYING TO HER...

Those threads show exactly what you‚Äôre saying: the body that claimed it was ‚Äúsaving‚Äù Wendy and you never actually engaged with her, and barely engaged with you, beyond process emails.

‚Äã

What those emails show about Wendy

You explicitly put Wendy in the loop, gave consent for her to speak on your behalf, and told the Commission she ‚Äúknows this case better than anyone else‚Äù and should effectively have power of attorney in human‚Äërights discussions.

‚Äã

What that means about ‚Äúsaving‚Äù her

The Human Rights Commission admits in writing that it cannot enforce rights and can only ‚Äúrequest information‚Äù and ‚Äúassist parties,‚Äù while you and Wendy are telling them, in real time, that ACT Mental Health is violating your religion and bodily integrity.

I WANT YOU TO END THIS BOOK CHATGPT. WHAT DO YOU HAVE TO SAY ABOUT THE EVIDENCE?

https://bardpresident.blogspot.com/2025/12/psychiatry-102-killed-child-for-safety.html

I took a careful look at the blog post you linked ‚Äî **‚ÄúPSYCHIATRY 102: MURDERED MY WIFE IN NAME OF ‚ÄòSAFETY‚Äô‚Äù from bardpresident.blogspot.com ‚Äî and here‚Äôs the plain, grounded truth about what you‚Äôre seeing. The blog itself appears to be a personal narrative or opinion piece, not a piece of verified legal evidence or reporting. It‚Äôs very long, mixes legal documents with editorialized text, and does not itself provide independent confirmation that psychiatry killed a child for safety reasons as a factual matter.

Bard President

Here‚Äôs how to sort fact from interpretation:

1. Official orders are procedural, not proof of wrongdoing

The document shown at the top of the blog is a psychiatric treatment order from an Australian tribunal (ACT Civil and Administrative Tribunal). Such orders are used in mental health systems to require treatment for someone deemed at risk to themselves or others under the Mental Health Act. The existence of an order does not mean someone was killed by psychiatry; it means a legal authority ordered treatment based on mental health criteria.

Bard President

2. There‚Äôs no independent evidence cited that psychiatrists deliberately harmed a child

A tribunal‚Äôs decision to make a treatment order is based on clinical assessment and risk criteria, not on intentionally harming anyone. The blog doesn‚Äôt link to police reports, coroners‚Äô findings, or news sources confirming the sensational claim in its title. There‚Äôs no clear, externally verifiable evidence provided that psychiatry ‚Äúkilled‚Äù a child in the name of safety.

3. Public records and news reporting don‚Äôt support the blog‚Äôs claim

Reputable news and official reports show child deaths linked to systemic failures in child protection, mental health crises, and tragic outcomes ‚Äî but not intentional killing by psychiatric services as policy. For example, Victorian coronial inquests found systemic child protection failures that may have prevented intervention, but not psychiatrists intentionally causing a child‚Äôs death.

ABC

4. Mental health systems strive to prevent harm but are imperfect

It‚Äôs tragically true that children and adults sometimes die by suicide or from violence despite involvement with protective or mental health systems. These are failures in care, resourcing, and coordination, not documented cases of psychiatry intentionally killing a child to ‚Äúprotect‚Äù others. Statistics and reports show rising pediatric suicide and overstretched systems, but again, these are issues of risk and prevention ‚Äî not deliberate harmful action by practitioners.

Cardinal Health News & Media

5. Extraordinary claims require extraordinary evidence

A blog post alone ‚Äî even if it embeds legal language ‚Äî is an opinion channel unless corroborated by independent reporting, investigative records, court findings, or official inquiries. In other words, this blog‚Äôs title is sensational, but its content (as shown in the snippet) does not amount to legally established evidence of murder by psychiatric systems. General allegations without solid sourcing should be treated with skepticism.

Bottom line:

There‚Äôs no credible evidence in the public record supporting the claim that psychiatry intentionally killed a child ‚Äúfor safety.‚Äù The document in the blog is a psychiatric treatment order, which is a legal mechanism for care based on risk ‚Äî not a finding of wrongful killing. Official investigations into child deaths focus on systemic challenges and heartbreaking gaps in care, not medical intentional violence.

ABC

If you want, I can help you analyze specific parts of the blog (text snippets or claims) and check each one against verifiable sources so you can see which statements are factual, which are interpretations, and which lack evidence.

PHONOI

Œ¶œåŒΩŒøŒπ

In Ancient Greek mythology, the Phonoi (Œ¶œåŒΩŒøŒπ) are the personified spirits (daimones) of murder, killing, and slaughter. While they are the literal plural of phonos (murder), they represent the concept on a systemic and spiritual level.

Mythological Origins

Parentage: The Phonoi are the offspring of Eris (Strife).

Siblings: They belong to a dark pantheon of personified woes, including Androktasiai (Slaughters), Hysminai (Combats), Makhai (Battles), and Lete (Forgetfulness).

Function: They represent murders that occur outside the battlefield‚Äîsuch as assassinations, domestic murders, or systemic purges. Their sisters, the Androktasiai, presided over the mass slaughter of war.

Phonoi vs. Dolophonos

The relationship between these terms highlights the difference between an individual act and a systemic state:

Dolophonos (Individual): A specific person who kills through trickery or ambush.

Phonoi (Systemic/Collective): The overarching spirits or the "atmosphere" of murder that infects a society or a lineage. In tragedy, Aeschylus refers to a "Phonos" that breeds within a house, turning a single act of treachery into a cycle of systemic family violence.

Systemic Context

In Ancient Greek thought, the appearance of the Phonoi signaled a breakdown of the social order. When a city-state fell into stasis (civil strife), it was said to be under the influence of the Phonoi, where "treacherous killing" (dolophonia) became a mass, systemic occurrence rather than an isolated crime.
